# Predicate-only weak sutras

Generated from the current `PaninianDerivationEngine` by routing every truth-gated sutra through its positive fixture. A sutra is listed here when its predicate accepts the fixture but the coordinator only traces, labels, falls back, errors, or produces no meaningful surface/state effect. This is a fix list, not a claim that the sutra is linguistically unimportant.

## Summary

- Total truth-gated sutras inspected: 3983
- Has concrete coordinator effect: 2091
- Predicate-only / weak: 1891
- Dispatcher errors: 1
- Total requiring upgrade: 1892
